(*
In this file, we define displayed left universal arrows and show how they define a left universal arrow for the corresponding total pseudo-functor.
Created by Kobe Wullaert at 06/12/2022.

Contents
1. Definition of a displayed universal arrow.
2. A make constructor when the 2-cells of the displayed bicategories are propositional.
3. A make constructor when the 2-cells of the displayed bicategories are propositional and groupoidal.
4. A make constructor when the 2-cells of the displayed bicategories are contractible.
*)

A: UU
B: A → UU
a1, a2: A
b1: B a1
b2: B a2
∏ p : a1,, b1 = a2,, b2,
b1 =
transportb B (base_paths (a1,, b1) (a2,, b2) p) b2


A: UU
B: A → UU
a1, a2: A
b1: B a1
b2: B a2
∏ p : a1,, b1 = a2,, b2,
b1 =
transportb B (base_paths (a1,, b1) (a2,, b2) p) b2

  
A: UU
B: A → UU
a1, a2: A
b1: B a1
b2: B a2
q: a1,, b1 = a2,, b2
b1 =
transportb B (base_paths (a1,, b1) (a2,, b2) q) b2

  
A: UU
B: A → UU
a1, a2: A
b1: B a1
b2: B a2
q: a1,, b1 = a2,, b2
transportf B (base_paths (a1,, b1) (a2,, b2) q) b1 =
b2

  apply (fiber_paths q).
Qed.

Section DisplayedLeftUniversalArrow.

  Context {B1 B2 : bicat}
          {R : psfunctor B1 B2}
          (LUR : left_universal_arrow R).

  Let L : B2 -> B1 := pr1 LUR.
  Let η : ∏ x : B2, B2 ⟦ x, R (L x) ⟧ := pr12 LUR.
  Let adj :  ∏ (x : B2) (y : B1), adj_equivalence_of_cats (left_universal_arrow_functor R x y η)
      := pr22 LUR.

  Context {D1 : disp_bicat B1} {D2 : disp_bicat B2}
          (RR : disp_psfunctor D1 D2 R).

  Definition disp_left_universal_arrow0 : UU
    := ∑ (LL : ∏ x : B2, D2 x → D1 (L x)),
       ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x),  xx -->[η x] (RR _ (LL _ xx)).

  Context (dLUR : disp_left_universal_arrow0).

  Let LL := pr1 dLUR.
  Let ηη := pr2 dLUR.

  Let η0 : ∏ x0 : total_bicat D2, total_bicat D2 ⟦ x0, (total_psfunctor D1 D2 R RR) (_,,LL (pr1 x0) (pr2 x0)) ⟧
    := λ x, η (pr1 x) ,, ηη _ (pr2 x).

  
B1, B2: bicat
R: psfunctor B1 B2
LUR: left_universal_arrow R
L:= pr1 LUR: B2 → B1
η:= pr12 LUR: ∏ x : B2, B2 ⟦ x, R (L x) ⟧
adj:= pr22 LUR: ∏ (x : B2) (y : B1),
adj_equivalence_of_cats (left_universal_arrow_functor R x y η)
D1: disp_bicat B1
D2: disp_bicat B2
RR: disp_psfunctor D1 D2 R
dLUR: disp_left_universal_arrow0
LL:= pr1 dLUR: ∏ x : B2, D2 x → D1 (L x)
ηη:= pr2 dLUR: (λ LL : ∏ x : B2, D2 x → D1 (L x),
 ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x),
 xx -->[ η x] RR (L x) (LL x xx)) 
  (pr1 dLUR)
η0:= λ x : total_bicat D2,
η (pr1 x),, ηη (pr1 x) (pr2 x): ∏ x0 : total_bicat D2,
total_bicat D2 ⟦ x0,
total_psfunctor D1 D2 R RR
  (L (pr1 x0),, LL (pr1 x0) (pr2 x0)) ⟧
x: B2
xx: D2 x
y: B1
yy: D1 y
disp_functor_data
  (left_universal_arrow_functor R x y η)
  (disp_hom (LL x xx) yy) (disp_hom xx (RR y yy))

y: B1
yy: D1 y
∏ (x0 y0 : hom (L x) y)
(xx0 : disp_hom (LL x xx) yy x0)
(yy0 : disp_hom (LL x xx) yy y0)
(f : hom (L x) y ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧),
xx0 -->[ f] yy0
→ ηη x xx ;; (♯ RR)%bicategory xx0 -->[
  (# (left_universal_arrow_functor R x y η))%cat f] 
  (ηη x xx ;; (♯ RR)%bicategory yy0)

  (L (pr1 x0),, LL (pr1 x0) (pr2 x0)) ⟧
x: B2
xx: D2 x
y: B1
yy: D1 y
f, g: hom (L x) y
ff: disp_hom (LL x xx) yy f
gg: disp_hom (LL x xx) yy g
α: hom (L x) y ⟦ f, g ⟧
αα: ff -->[ α] gg
ηη x xx ;; (♯ RR)%bicategory ff -->[
(# (left_universal_arrow_functor R x y η))%cat α] 
(ηη x xx ;; (♯ RR)%bicategory gg)

    exact (disp_lwhisker (ηη _ xx) (disp_psfunctor_cell _ _ _ RR αα)).
  Defined.

adj_equivalence_of_cats (left_universal_arrow_functor R x y η)
D1: disp_bicat B1
D2: disp_bicat B2
RR: disp_psfunctor D1 D2 R
dLUR: disp_left_universal_arrow0
LL:= pr1 dLUR: ∏ x : B2, D2 x → D1 (L x)
ηη:= pr2 dLUR: (λ LL : ∏ x : B2, D2 x → D1 (L x),
 ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x),
 xx -->[ η x] RR (L x) (LL x xx)) 
  (pr1 dLUR)
η0:= λ x : total_bicat D2,
η (pr1 x),, ηη (pr1 x) (pr2 x): ∏ x0 : total_bicat D2,
total_bicat D2 ⟦ x0,
total_psfunctor D1 D2 R RR
  (L (pr1 x0),, LL (pr1 x0) (pr2 x0)) ⟧
x: B2
xx: D2 x
y: B1
yy: D1 y
lur:= left_universal_arrow_functor
  (total_psfunctor D1 D2 R RR) 
  (x,, xx) (y,, yy) η0: hom
  ((λ x0 : total_bicat D2,
    L (pr1 x0),, LL (pr1 x0) (pr2 x0)) 
     (x,, xx)) (y,, yy)
⟶ hom (x,, xx)

   •• pr2 ((# (pr1 lur))%cat (β,, ββ))) =

        hh))

     α β)

  Definition disp_left_universal_arrow_functor
             {x : B2} (xx : D2 x) {y : B1} (yy : D1 y)
    : disp_functor (left_universal_arrow_functor R x y η) (disp_hom (LL _ xx) yy) (disp_hom xx (RR _ yy))
    := _ ,, disp_left_universal_arrow_is_functor xx yy.

  Definition disp_left_universal_arrow_universality : UU
    := ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x) (y : B1) (yy : D1 y),
      is_equiv_over (_ ,, adj x y) (disp_left_universal_arrow_functor xx yy).

η0:= λ x : total_bicat D2,
η (pr1 x),, ηη (pr1 x) (pr2 x): ∏ x0 : total_bicat D2,
total_bicat D2 ⟦ x0,
total_psfunctor D1 D2 R RR
  (L (pr1 x0),, LL (pr1 x0) (pr2 x0)) ⟧
dLURu: disp_left_universal_arrow_universality
x: B2
xx: D2 x
y: B1
yy: D1 y
adj_equivalence_of_cats
  (total_functor
     (disp_left_universal_arrow_functor xx yy))
 exact (total_adj_equivalence_of_cats (dLURu x xx y yy)).
  Defined.

End DisplayedLeftUniversalArrow.

Section DisplayedLeftUniversalArrowDef.

  Context {B1 B2 : bicat}
          {R : psfunctor B1 B2}
          (LUR : left_universal_arrow R)
          {D1 : disp_bicat B1} {D2 : disp_bicat B2}
          (RR : disp_psfunctor D1 D2 R).

  Let L : B2 -> B1 := pr1 LUR.
  Let η : ∏ x : B2, B2 ⟦ x, R (L x) ⟧ := pr12 LUR.
  Let adj :  ∏ (x : B2) (y : B1), adj_equivalence_of_cats (left_universal_arrow_functor R x y η)
      := pr22 LUR.

  Definition disp_left_universal_arrow : UU
    := ∑ (LL : ∏ x : B2, D2 x → D1 (L x)),
      ∑ ηη : ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x),  xx -->[η x] (RR _ (LL _ xx)),
        ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x) (y : B1) (yy : D1 y),
        is_equiv_over (_ ,, adj x y)
                      (disp_left_universal_arrow_functor LUR RR (LL,,ηη) xx yy).

  Definition total_left_universal_arrow
             (dLUR : disp_left_universal_arrow)
    : left_universal_arrow (total_psfunctor D1 D2 R RR)
    := total_disp_left_universal_arrow LUR RR (pr1 dLUR ,, pr12 dLUR) (pr22 dLUR).

End DisplayedLeftUniversalArrowDef.

Section MakeDisplayedLeftUniversalArrowIfPropositional.

  Context {B1 B2 : bicat}
          {R : psfunctor B1 B2}
          (LUR : left_universal_arrow R)
          {D1 : disp_bicat B1} {D2 : disp_bicat B2}
          (RR : disp_psfunctor D1 D2 R)
          (D1_2cells_prop : disp_2cells_isaprop D1)
          (D2_2cells_prop : disp_2cells_isaprop D2).

  Let L : B2 -> B1 := pr1 LUR.
  Let η : ∏ x : B2, B2 ⟦ x, R (L x) ⟧ := pr12 LUR.
  Let adj :  ∏ (x : B2) (y : B1), adj_equivalence_of_cats (left_universal_arrow_functor R x y η)
      := pr22 LUR.

  Context (LL : ∏ x : B2, D2 x → D1 (L x))
    (ηη : ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x),  xx -->[η x] (RR _ (LL _ xx))).

  Context (LL_mor : ∏ x xx y yy f (ff : xx -->[ f] RR y yy),
              LL x xx -->[ right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y) f] yy).
  Context (LL_2cell : ∏ x xx y yy (f1 f2 : B2 ⟦ x, R y ⟧)
                      (ff1 : xx -->[ f1] RR y yy) (ff2 : xx -->[ f2] RR y yy)
                      (α : f1 ==> f2),
              ff1 ==>[α] ff2
              → (LL_mor x xx y yy f1 ff1) ==>[(# (right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y)))%cat α]
                  (LL_mor x xx y yy f2 ff2)).
  Context (LL_unit : ∏ x xx y yy f ff,
              ff ==>[adjunit (adj x y) f]
                (LL_mor x xx y yy (η x · (# R)%cat f) (ηη x xx ;; disp_psfunctor_mor D1 D2 R RR ff))).

  Context (LL_unit_inv : ∏ x xx y yy f ff,
        (LL_mor x xx y yy ((pr12 LUR) x · (# R)%cat f) (ηη x xx ;; disp_psfunctor_mor D1 D2 R RR ff))
          ==>[inv_from_z_iso (unit_pointwise_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence (adj x y) _)] ff).

  Context (LL_counit : ∏ x xx y yy f ff,
              (ηη x xx ;; disp_psfunctor_mor D1 D2 R RR (LL_mor x xx y yy f ff))
                ==>[adjcounit (adj x y) f] ff).

  Context (LL_counit_inv : ∏ x xx y yy f ff,
              ff ==>[inv_from_z_iso (counit_pointwise_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence (adj x y) _)]
                (ηη x xx ;; disp_psfunctor_mor D1 D2 R RR (LL_mor x xx y yy f ff))).

D2_2cells_prop: disp_2cells_isaprop D2
L:= pr1 LUR: B2 → B1
η:= pr12 LUR: ∏ x : B2, B2 ⟦ x, R (L x) ⟧
adj:= pr22 LUR: ∏ (x : B2) (y : B1),
adj_equivalence_of_cats
  (left_universal_arrow_functor R x y η)
LL: ∏ x : B2, D2 x → D1 (L x)
ηη: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x),
xx -->[ η x] RR (L x) (LL x xx)
LL_mor: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : pr1 D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y) 
(f : B2 ⟦ x, R y ⟧),
xx -->[ f] RR y yy
→ LL x xx -->[
  right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y) f] yy
LL_2cell: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : pr1 D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y)
(f1 f2 : B2 ⟦ x, R y ⟧)
(ff1 : xx -->[ f1] RR y yy)
(ff2 : xx -->[ f2] RR y yy)
(α : f1 ==> f2),
ff1 ==>[ α] ff2
→ LL_mor x xx y yy f1 ff1 ==>[
  (# (right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y)))%cat
    α] LL_mor x xx y yy f2 ff2
LL_unit: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : pr1 D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y) 
(f : hom (L x) y)
(ff : LL x xx -->[
      functor_identity (hom (L x) y) f] yy),
ff ==>[
adjunit (adj x y) f] 
LL_mor x xx y yy (η x · (# R)%cat f)
  (ηη x xx ;; (♯ RR)%bicategory ff)
LL_unit_inv: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : pr1 D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y)
(f : B1 ⟦ pr1 LUR x, y ⟧)
(ff : LL x xx -->[ f] yy),
LL_mor x xx y yy
  ((pr12 LUR) x · (# R)%cat f)
  (ηη x xx ;; (♯ RR)%bicategory ff) ==>[
inv_from_z_iso
  (unit_pointwise_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence
     (adj x y) f)] ff
LL_counit: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y) 
(f : hom x (R y))
(ff : xx -->[ f] RR y yy),
ηη x xx ;; (♯ RR)%bicategory
             (LL_mor x xx y yy f ff) ==>[
adjcounit (adj x y) f] ff
LL_counit_inv: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y)
(f : B2 ⟦ x, R y ⟧)
(ff : xx -->[ f] RR y yy),
ff ==>[
inv_from_z_iso
  (counit_pointwise_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence
     (adj x y) f)] ηη x xx ;; 
(♯ RR)%bicategory
  (LL_mor x xx y yy f ff)

xx: D2 x
y: B1
yy: D1 y
(λ b : disp_nat_trans_data
         (adjcounit
            (left_universal_arrow_functor R x y
               (pr12 LUR),, 
             (pr22 LUR) x y))
         (disp_functor_composite
            (make_disp_functor_if_prop xx yy)

  right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y) f] yy

  (# (right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y)))%cat
    α] LL_mor x xx y yy f2 ff2

Section MakeDisplayedLeftUniversalArrowIfGroupoidalAndProp.

  Context {B1 B2 : bicat}
          {R : psfunctor B1 B2}
          (LUR : left_universal_arrow R)
          {D1 : disp_bicat B1} {D2 : disp_bicat B2}
          (RR : disp_psfunctor D1 D2 R)
          (D1_2cells_grp : disp_locally_groupoid D1)
          (D2_2cells_grp : disp_locally_groupoid D2)
          (D1_2cells_prop : disp_2cells_isaprop D1)
          (D2_2cells_prop : disp_2cells_isaprop D2).

  Let L : B2 -> B1 := pr1 LUR.
  Let η : ∏ x : B2, B2 ⟦ x, R (L x) ⟧ := pr12 LUR.
  Let adj :  ∏ (x : B2) (y : B1), adj_equivalence_of_cats (left_universal_arrow_functor R x y η)
      := pr22 LUR.

  Context (LL : ∏ x : B2, D2 x → D1 (L x))
    (ηη : ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x),  xx -->[η x] (RR _ (LL _ xx))).

  Context (LL_mor : ∏ x xx y yy f (ff : xx -->[ f] RR y yy),
              LL x xx -->[ right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y) f] yy).
  Context (LL_2cell : ∏ x xx y yy (f1 f2 : B2 ⟦ x, R y ⟧)
                      (ff1 : xx -->[ f1] RR y yy) (ff2 : xx -->[ f2] RR y yy)
                      (α : f1 ==> f2),
              ff1 ==>[α] ff2
              → (LL_mor x xx y yy f1 ff1) ==>[(# (right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y)))%cat α]
                  (LL_mor x xx y yy f2 ff2)
          ).
  Context (LL_unit : ∏ x xx y yy f ff,
        ff ==>[adjunit (adj x y) f]
    (LL_mor x xx y yy (η x · (# R)%cat f) (ηη x xx ;; disp_psfunctor_mor D1 D2 R RR ff))).

  Context (LL_counit : ∏ x xx y yy f ff,
        (ηη x xx ;; disp_psfunctor_mor D1 D2 R RR (LL_mor x xx y yy f ff))
          ==>[adjcounit (adj x y) f] ff).

  (ηη x xx ;; (♯ RR)%bicategory ff)
LL_counit: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y) 
(f : hom x (R y))
(ff : xx -->[ f] RR y yy),
ηη x xx ;; (♯ RR)%bicategory
             (LL_mor x xx y yy f ff) ==>[
adjcounit (adj x y) f] ff

  right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y) f] yy

  (# (right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y)))%cat
    α] LL_mor x xx y yy f2 ff2

RR: disp_psfunctor D1 D2 R
D1_2cells_grp: disp_locally_groupoid D1
D2_2cells_grp: disp_locally_groupoid D2
D1_2cells_prop: disp_2cells_isaprop D1
D2_2cells_prop: disp_2cells_isaprop D2
L:= pr1 LUR: B2 → B1
η:= pr12 LUR: ∏ x : B2, B2 ⟦ x, R (L x) ⟧
adj:= pr22 LUR: ∏ (x : B2) (y : B1),
adj_equivalence_of_cats
  (left_universal_arrow_functor R x y η)
LL: ∏ x : B2, D2 x → D1 (L x)
ηη: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x),
xx -->[ η x] RR (L x) (LL x xx)
LL_mor: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : pr1 D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y) 
(f : B2 ⟦ x, R y ⟧),
xx -->[ f] RR y yy
→ LL x xx -->[
  right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y) f] yy
LL_2cell: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : pr1 D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y)
(f1 f2 : B2 ⟦ x, R y ⟧)
(ff1 : xx -->[ f1] RR y yy)
(ff2 : xx -->[ f2] RR y yy)
(α : f1 ==> f2),
ff1 ==>[ α] ff2
→ LL_mor x xx y yy f1 ff1 ==>[
  (# (right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y)))%cat
    α] LL_mor x xx y yy f2 ff2
LL_unit: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : pr1 D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y) 
(f : hom (L x) y)
(ff : LL x xx -->[
      functor_identity (hom (L x) y) f] yy),
ff ==>[
adjunit (adj x y) f] 
LL_mor x xx y yy (η x · (# R)%cat f)
  (ηη x xx ;; (♯ RR)%bicategory ff)
LL_counit: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y) 
(f : hom x (R y))
(ff : xx -->[ f] RR y yy),
ηη x xx ;; (♯ RR)%bicategory
             (LL_mor x xx y yy f ff) ==>[
adjcounit (adj x y) f] ff
∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y) 
(f : hom x (R y)) (ff : xx -->[ f] RR y yy),
?ηη x xx ;; (♯ RR)%bicategory (?LL_mor x xx y yy f ff) ==>[
adjcounit ((pr22 LUR) x y) f] ff

D1_2cells_prop: disp_2cells_isaprop D1
D2_2cells_prop: disp_2cells_isaprop D2
L:= pr1 LUR: B2 → B1
η:= pr12 LUR: ∏ x : B2, B2 ⟦ x, R (L x) ⟧
adj:= pr22 LUR: ∏ (x : B2) (y : B1),
adj_equivalence_of_cats
  (left_universal_arrow_functor R x y η)
LL: ∏ x : B2, D2 x → D1 (L x)
ηη: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x),
xx -->[ η x] RR (L x) (LL x xx)
LL_mor: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : pr1 D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y) 
(f : B2 ⟦ x, R y ⟧),
xx -->[ f] RR y yy
→ LL x xx -->[
  right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y) f] yy
LL_2cell: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : pr1 D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y)
(f1 f2 : B2 ⟦ x, R y ⟧)
(ff1 : xx -->[ f1] RR y yy)
(ff2 : xx -->[ f2] RR y yy)
(α : f1 ==> f2),
ff1 ==>[ α] ff2
→ LL_mor x xx y yy f1 ff1 ==>[
  (# (right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y)))%cat
    α] LL_mor x xx y yy f2 ff2
LL_unit: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : pr1 D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y) 
(f : hom (L x) y)
(ff : LL x xx -->[
      functor_identity (hom (L x) y) f] yy),
ff ==>[
adjunit (adj x y) f] 
LL_mor x xx y yy (η x · (# R)%cat f)
  (ηη x xx ;; (♯ RR)%bicategory ff)
LL_counit: ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x) 
(y : B1) (yy : D1 y) 
(f : hom x (R y))
(ff : xx -->[ f] RR y yy),
ηη x xx ;; (♯ RR)%bicategory
             (LL_mor x xx y yy f ff) ==>[
adjcounit (adj x y) f] ff
∏ (x : B2) (xx : pr1 D2 x) (y : B1) (yy : D1 y)
(f : B1 ⟦ pr1 LUR x, y ⟧) (ff : LL x xx -->[ f] yy),
LL_mor x xx y yy ((pr12 LUR) x · (# R)%cat f)
  (ηη x xx ;; (♯ RR)%bicategory ff) ==>[
inv_from_z_iso
  (unit_pointwise_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence
     ((pr22 LUR) x y) f)] ff

          {R : psfunctor B1 B2}
          (LUR : left_universal_arrow R)

          (RR : disp_psfunctor D1 D2 R)
          (D1_2cells_contr : disp_2cells_iscontr D1)
          (D2_2cells_contr : disp_2cells_iscontr D2).

  Let L : B2 -> B1 := pr1 LUR.
  Let η : ∏ x : B2, B2 ⟦ x, R (L x) ⟧ := pr12 LUR.
  Let adj :  ∏ (x : B2) (y : B1), adj_equivalence_of_cats (left_universal_arrow_functor R x y η)
      := pr22 LUR.

  Context (LL : ∏ x : B2, D2 x → D1 (L x))
    (ηη : ∏ (x : B2) (xx : D2 x),  xx -->[η x] (RR _ (LL _ xx))).

  Context (LL_mor : ∏ x xx y yy f (ff : xx -->[ f] RR y yy),
              LL x xx -->[ right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y) f] yy).

(ff2 : xx -->[ f2] RR y yy) 
(α : f1 ==> f2),
ff1 ==>[ α] ff2
→ ?LL_mor x xx y yy f1 ff1 ==>[
  (# (right_adjoint ((pr22 LUR) x y)))%cat α] 
  ?LL_mor x xx y yy f2 ff2
